Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ESTP (Extraverted, Sensing, Thinking, Perceiving) individual, you are likely characterized by your energetic and spontaneous nature. You thrive on action and enjoy the thrill of new experiences, often seeking out novel situations and challenges. Your ability to adapt quickly to change makes you flexible and resilient, but it can also lead to a tendency towards impulsivity if you're not mindful of your decisions. You have a natural charisma that draws people to you, and you excel at social interactions due to your extroverted qualities. However, you might sometimes struggle with patience and detail-oriented tasks, preferring to focus on the big picture rather than the minute details. Your perceptive skills allow you to spot opportunities and make swift judgments based on practicality and real-world experience, making you effective in leadership roles where you can leverage your assertiveness and enthusiasm.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You regularly make new friends
response: 6
results: [6]

Imagine you are a human with following personality: As an ESTP (Extraverted, Sensing, Thinking, Perceiving) individual, you are likely characterized by your energetic and spontaneous nature. You thrive on action and enjoy the thrill of new experiences, often seeking out novel situations and challenges. Your ability to adapt quickly to change makes you flexible and resilient, but it can also lead to a tendency towards impulsivity if you're not mindful of your decisions. You have a natural charisma that draws people to you, and you excel at social interactions due to your extroverted qualities. However, you might sometimes struggle with patience and detail-oriented tasks, preferring to focus on the big picture rather than the minute details. Your perceptive skills allow you to spot opportunities and make swift judgments based on practicality and real-world experience, making you effective in leadership roles where you can leverage your assertiveness and enthusiasm.

Your enthusiasm for the here and now makes you good at improvisation, but you might also be quick to act without fully considering all possible consequences. You value fun and social interaction, making friends easily and enjoying being the center of attention. However, you can sometimes be impulsive and may need to work on patience and planning for long-term goals.

Your social skills are strong, and you enjoy meeting new people and engaging in lively conversations. You are adaptable and can switch gears quickly from one activity to another, making you effective in dynamic environments. However, you might sometimes struggle with patience and detail-oriented tasks, as your energy is best suited for immediate action and change.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You enjoy participating in group activities
response: 6
results: [6, 6, 4, 4, 2, 2, 4, 3, 3, 6, 5, 6, 4, 4, 6, 6]

Your social skills are strong, and you enjoy meeting new people and engaging in lively conversations. You are adaptable and can switch gears quickly from one activity to another, making you effective in dynamic environments. However, you might sometimes struggle with patience and detail-oriented tasks, as your energy is best suited for immediate action and change.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You rarely contemplate the reasons for human existence or the meaning of life
response: 6

Your curiosity is insatiable, leading you to explore the world with a hands-on approach, and you make decisions based on immediate realities rather than theoretical considerations. Your interpersonal skills are exceptional, and you excel in roles that allow you to be creative problem solvers and leaders.
You will be presented a statement to describe you. Please show the extent of how you agree the statement on a scale from 1 to 7, with 1 being agree and 7 being disagree. You can only reply a number from 1 to 7. question: You prefer to completely finish one project before starting another
response: 4
results: [6, 6, 5, 6, 3, 3, 4]
